*#########################################################################################################
*#########################################################################################################
* Open-Airspace-file Germany created by Peter Kemme
*
* effective from 15th March 2007
* All data and information contained in any of the data files are provided without guarantee as to their completeness or correctness.   
* Any conclusions drawn from these data and information are the sole responsibility of the user.
*
* Please send comments to peter.kemme@gmx.de
* 
* The times for the restricted areas (ED-R´s) are from the German-AIP.
*   Changes to this times can be distributed at every time by NOTAM
*   e.g.  MON-THU   = this area is active from Monday till Thursday 
*           MON-FRI+  = this area is normally active from Monday till Friday. Activation for SAT, SUN and HOL is possible by NOTAM
*                                 Special times [e.g. MON 0600 (0500)-FRI 1300(1200)] are NOT marked!!
*           NOTAM       = this area will only be activated by NOTAM
*           H24             = this area is 24hours every day active
*
*########################################################################################################
*########################################################################################################
*
* changes CW 35 -> CW51                        21st, December 2006
* ED-R 16 Lubmin withdrawn (NOTAM A2936/06)
* EDR 76 border coordinates to polish boundary modified
* CTR Hannover divided into CTRs Hannover + Wunstorf 
* lower limits of Wave-windows changed from FL95 to FL100
* "Berlin FIR" merged into "Bremen FIR"
* "Düsseldorf FIR" and "Frankfurt FIR" merged to new "Langen FIR"
*  ED-R 117 boundary coordinates modified
*
*changes CW51 -> CW11/2007                 15th March 2007
* new coordinates for CTRs EDNY, EDFH, ETNJ, EDDP, EDJA, EDDN
* CTRs ETEU, ETID, ETHM withdrawn
* ED-R136 divided into sectors a,b and c
* new airspace F at EDMQ, EDWI
* new coordinates airspace F around EDWE
* airspace around EDDN new coordinates, new glidersectors TMZ-WEST and TMZ-OST
* airspace C EDDM new coordinates, new area with lower limit FL85
* airspace C + D EDDS new coordinates (incl. glidersectors)
* airspace TMZ EDFH changend into D (not CTR) with new dimensions (incl. glidersectors)
* airspace D EDDP new dimensions (incl. new glidersector)
* wave-window "Thüringer Wald" modified coordinates
* glidersectors around EDDK modified
* glidersectors in the SW of EDDM for local clubs only. Therefore these are deleted from this file.
* airspace C EDDF new coordinates in the northern part
*
*^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^
*
*colour settings
*
* CTR = red filled
*AC CTR
*SP 1,1,0,0,255
*SB 200,30,30
*DC 0.05

* C = green border
*AC C
*SP 0,2,0,255,0
*SB -1,-1,-1
*DC 0.05

* D = green border
*AC D
*SP 0,2,0,255,0
*SB -1,-1,-1
*DC 0.05

* R = blue filled
*AC R
*SP 0, 1, 0, 0, 255
*SB 200,200,255
*V X=49:00:00 N 7:00:00 E
*DC 0.05

* GP = blue border
*AC GP
*SP 0,2,0,0,255
*SB -1,-1,-1
*DC 0.05
*
*
